FG.BP TMPCP
New record
----: I PROGRAM TMPCP
Bottom at line 1
----: I ECHO OFF
Bottom at line 2
----: I DUMMY=@(0,0)
Bottom at line 3
----: I INPUT TMPS,30000:
Bottom at line 4
----: I OPEN "FG.BP" TO MYFILE THEN
Bottom at line 5
----: I WRITE TMPS ON MYFILE,"TMPBCP"
Bottom at line 6
----: I CLOSE MYFILE
Bottom at line 7
